Everywhere again they discuss news about the ban on cryptocurrencies. At first I did not want to comment on this at all. The bottom line is: neither the Central Bank nor any other organization has influence on bitcoin. For some other cryptocurrencies - it is possible, but with bitcoin everything is definitely and understandable. A little story: there was a time when there was a high tax on the purchase/sale of dollars. And almost every branch of Sberbank (and there were almost no others then) there was a car with an enlarged photocopy of the dollar on the windshield. These were changing - the prototype of modern exchangers is crypts. Only in those days there was almost no Internet, and there was no online banking at all. What is the result: the Central Bank, Fed, CIA, KGB or anyone can throw anything and try to ban anything, but Bitcoin was created precisely taking into account such prohibitions. There are no technologies (and is not expected) that will allow all impostors even try to ban cryptocurrencies. All that the Central Bank can do: to ban P2P transfers (from a client to the client) in online banking and run to catch a change. Will they do it? If they do, then we will discuss the prohibitions. And in all other cases, this is an informational noise that they let them leave. Do not waste time on excess noise is how to discuss the ban on lace panties (there was such an initiative too, yeah).

I ran my eyes with the main theses of the three sources: the news from Bloomberg and the conference from the representative of the Central Bank is a mud, which is not even worth the fraction of attention. Regarding Binance - I‚Äôll say once again - they are in full cooperation and there is an official representative in the Russian Federation. All data will be transmitted to the authorities - this is a matter of time. If there is a ban, they will give the funds. Such cases have already been more than once. But it is better not to store significant amounts on exchanges.
